I wanna caution people who wanna try this. I wrote down my dreams for a while years ago. My dreams became super vivid, they were always good or just bizarre, and it got to the point where I started questioning in my dream if I was dreaming. Flash forward a few years and mental health issues and my dreams are still super vivid, but now they're nightmares and they feel real. Half the time they're just too realistic to shake off and I wake up upset and disturbed and yes I'm talking to my therapist about it. So, yeah, you know your headspace better than anyone, but if you want vivid dreams, just be mindful that nightmares are dreams too and it will work the same way. Have fun, but stay safe ğŸ’œ
